 3828  \t{ \n\t\t// Number of subsequences with substring \n\t\t// str[0..i-1] \n\t\tdp[i] = 2*dp[i-1]; \n\n\t\t// If current character has appeared \n\t\t// before, then remove all subsequences \n\t\t// ending with previous occurrence. \n\t\tif (last[str[i-1]] != -1) \n\t\t\tdp[i] = dp[i] - dp[last[str[i-1]]]; \n\n\t\t// Mark occurrence of current character \n\t\tlast[str[i-1]] = (i-1); \n\t}
